### agentmemory - Beginner Analysis — `03 Projects/agentmemory - Beginner Analysis/`

**v66 agentmemory** (2026-05-14 session 73++): **T2 Service — FIRST dedicated agent-memory-system in the 65-wiki corpus**; **FIRST wiki built under routine v2.2**. `rohitg00/agentmemory` — *"Persistent memory for AI coding agents, powered by iii-engine's three primitives."* Solo author Rohit Ghumare; 7,900 stars / 675 forks / **~35 days old (first release 2026-04-09) / ~226 stars/day** (HIGH velocity, just below the 300/day EXTREME-VIRAL flag; drive-by-stars-dominant engagement profile); Apache-2.0; TypeScript 82.4%; `@agentmemory/agentmemory` v0.9.12 on npm. Architecture: **4-tier memory consolidation** (Working→Episodic→Semantic→Procedural, Ebbinghaus decay) + **triple-stream RRF search** (BM25+Vector+Graph) + **12 auto-capture hooks** + 51 MCP tools + 107 REST endpoints + 15+ agent platforms. **PRIMARY: NEW Pattern #85 Platform-Primitive Foundation N=1 stale-flagged** — corpus-first: built ENTIRELY on iii-engine's primitives, self-identifies as *"a running iii instance,"* delegates ALL infrastructure, counts in host units, extends via host CLI; 4 promotion criteria; coupling-risk built into definition; full proposal-document at `03 Projects/agentmemory - Beginner Analysis/01 Analysis/(C) Pattern Platform-Primitive Foundation N=1 registration proposal.md`. **NEW Pattern #18 sub-archetype: shared-backend-service** (one server, 15+ platforms as clients — 3rd multi-platform mechanism after Layer 1 coexistence + Layer 2 translation). **NEW observational candidate: AI-Generated-Repo Artifact Contamination** (DESIGN.md ships 288 lines of unrelated "Lamborghini design system" boilerplate — verified 3 ways: 2 WebFetch + raw curl — corpus-first provably-contaminated governance file; bundled with viral-velocity-outpacing-quality-maturity observation; counter-evidence vs Pattern #12 file-count proxy). **6 within-pattern strengthenings**: Pattern #8 first memory-retrieval-domain benchmark (LongMemEval-S ICLR 2025, 95.2% R@5) + Pattern #28 STRONG dual-axis multi-provider (LLM + embeddings) + Pattern #12 counter-evidence + Pattern #81 "names-the-drift-and-drifts-anyway" + Pattern #83 MIXED partial evidence (**NOT a clean N=3** — README over-claims while CHANGELOG/ROADMAP honest) + Pattern #19/#57. **Pattern #52 OBSERVATIONAL watch** (v69 sustained-velocity re-check). **Storm Bear meta-entity Phase 0.9 4-of-4 STRICT PASS → STRONG INCLUDE** — FIRST 4/4 in the post-amendment window; streak → 2; 10-instance window v57-v66 = 80% INCLUDE. **Highest-relevance pilot candidate in recent corpus** — persistent memory for the vault's own Claude Code substrate; recommended as a FENCED pilot (scratch project → read-mostly vault → decision gate), NOT a substrate swap; the vault has already hit the failure mode agentmemory targets (584 KB CLAUDE.md refactor). **7 corpus-firsts.** Sibling to vault project graphify (knowledge-graph search stream). State: 26 → **27 active** / 0.605 → **0.628 ratio**; **v68 stale-checks: Pattern #85 + Pattern #18 shared-backend-service sub-archetype**; v68/v69 AI-Generated-Repo Contamination observational; v69 Pattern #52 sustained-velocity. ⚠️ Build note: `DESIGN.md` content-contamination is a real repo artifact, NOT a fetch error — excluded as a source per "NEVER fabricate" discipline.
